's' : '') + ' offline');\n    } else {\n      var names = [];\n      for (var i = 0; i < blobs.length; i++) {\n        var p = blobs[i].person;\n        if (p && names.indexOf(p) === -1) names.push(p);\n      }\n      if (names.length > 0) {\n        setBanner('ok', 'All clear — ' + names.length + ' people home, ' +\n                   online.length + ' devices online');\n      } else {\n        setBanner('ok', 'All clear — No one detected, ' + online.length + ' devices online');\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // ── Snapshot processing ──\n\n  function handleSnapshot(snapshot) {\n    cached = {\n      blobs: snapshot.blobs || [],\n      nodes: snapshot.nodes || [],\n      zones: snapshot.zones || [],\n      triggers: snapshot.triggers || [],\n      events: snapshot.events || [],\n      confidence: snapshot.confidence,\n      security_mode: snapshot.security_mode,\n      briefing: snapshot.briefing,\n      anomaly_active: snapshot.anomaly_active,\n    };\n\n    if (snapshot.events && snapshot.events.length > 0) {\n      recentEvents = snapshot.events.slice(0, 5);\n    }\n\n    updateBanner();\n    updatePeopleCard();\n    updateDevicesCard();\n    updateEventsCard();\n    updateExtras();\n  }\n\n  function handleIncremental(msg) {\n    mergeIncremental(msg);\n\n    if (msg.events && msg.events.length > 0) {\n      recentEvents = msg.events.concat(recentEvents).slice(0, 5);\n    }\n\n    // Always refresh all cards from cached state\n    updateBanner();\n    updatePeopleCard();\n    updateDevicesCard();\n    updateEventsCard();\n    updateExtras();\n  }\n\n  // ── WebSocket ──\n\n  function connect() {\n    var proto = location.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss:' : 'ws:';\n    var url   = proto + '//' + location.host + '/ws/dashboard';\n    ws = new WebSocket(url);\n\n    ws.onopen = function () {\n      reconnectDelay = 1000;\n    };\n\n    ws.onmessage = function (evt) {\n      var msg;\n      try { msg = JSON.parse(evt.data); } catch (e) { return; }\n\n      if (msg.type === 'snapshot') {\n        handleSnapshot(msg);\n      } else {\n        handleIncremental(msg);\n      }\n    };\n\n    ws.onclose = function () {\n      setBanner('warn', 'Reconnecting&hellip;');\n      setTimeout(function () {\n        reconnectDelay = Math.min(reconnectDelay * 2, 10000);\n        connect();\n      }, reconnectDelay);\n    };\n\n    ws.onerror = function () {\n      ws.close();\n    };\n  }\n\n  // ── Boot ──\n  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {\n    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', connect);\n  } else {\n    connect();\n  }\n\n  // Refresh relative timestamps every 30s\n  setInterval(updateEventsCard, 30000);\n})();\n","numLines":301,"startLine":1,"totalLines":301}}}

      zones: [],\n35\t        blobs: [],\n36\t        nodes: [],\n37\t        events: [],\n38\t        alerts: [],\n39\t        system: {\n40\t            detection_quality: 0,\n41\t            security_mode: false,\n42\t            nodes_online: 0,\n43\t            nodes_total: 0\n44\t        },\n45\t\n46\t        // UI state\n47\t        filters: {\n48\t            eventTypes: ['presence', 'zone_entry', 'zone_exit', 'alert', 'system'],\n49\t            person: '',\n50\t            zone: ''\n51\t        },\n52\t\n53\t        // Sleep data\n54\t        sleepData: null,\n55\t\n56\t        // Alert dismissal state\n57\t        silencedUntil: null\n58\t    };\n59\t\n60\t    // ============================================\n61\t    // DOM Elements\n62\t    // ============================================\n63\t    const dom = {};\n64\t\n65\t    function initDOM() {\n66\t        dom.connectionStatus = document.getElementById('connection-status');\n67\t        dom.alertBanner = document.getElementById('alert-banner');\n68\t        dom.alertTitle = document.getElementById('alert-title');\n69\t        dom.alertMessage = document.getElementById('alert-message');\n70\t        dom.alertDismiss = document.getElementById('alert-dismiss');\n71\t        dom.zonesGrid = document.getElementById('zones-grid');\n72\t        dom.activityFeed = document.getElementById('activity-feed');\n73\t        dom.modeToggle = document.getElementById('mode-toggle');\n74\t        dom.securityBtn = document.getElementById('action-security');\n75\t        dom.securityLabel = document.getElementById('security-label');\n76\t        dom.rebaselineBtn = document.getElementById('action-rebaseline');\n77\t        dom.silenceBtn = document.getElementById('action-silence');\n78\t        dom.sleepCard = document.getElementById('sleep-card');\n79\t        dom.sleepContent = document.getElementById('sleep-content');\n80\t        dom.systemStatus = document.getElementById('system-status');\n81\t    }\n82\t\n83\t    // ============================================\n84\t    // WebSocket Connection\n85\t    // ============================================\n86\t    function connectWebSocket() {\n87\t        if (state.ws && state.ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {\n88\t            return;\n89\t        }\n90\t\n91\t        updateConnectionStatus('connecting');\n92\t\n93\t        try {\n94\t            state.ws = new WebSocket(CONFIG.WS_URL);\n95\t        } catch (e) {\n96\t            console.error('[Simple Mode] Failed to create WebSocket:', e);\n97\t            scheduleReconnect();\n98\t            return;\n99\t        }\n100\t\n101\t        state.ws.onopen = function() {\n102\t            state.connected = true;\n103\t            state.reconnectAttempts = 0;\n104\t            updateConnectionStatus('connected');\n105\t            console.log('[Simple Mode] WebSocket connected');\n106\t        };\n107\t\n108\t        state.ws.onclose = function(event) {\n109\t            state.connected = false;\n110\t            updateConnectionStatus('disconnected');\n111\t            console.log('[Simple Mode] WebSocket closed:', event.code, event.reason);\n112\t            scheduleReconnect();\n113\t        };\n114\t\n115\t        state.ws.onerror = function(error) {\n116\t            console.error('[Simple Mode] WebSocket error:', error);\n117\t        };\n118\t\n119\t        state.ws.onmessage = function(event) {\n120\t            handleMessage(event.data);\n121\t        };\n122\t    }\n123\t\n124\t    function scheduleReconnect() {\n125\t        if (state.reconnectTimer) {\n126\t            clearTimeout(state.reconnectTimer);\n127\t        }\n128\t\n129\t        const delay = Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, state.reconnectAttempts), 10000);\n130\t        state.reconnectAttempts++;\n131\t\n132\t        console.log('[Simple Mode] Reconnecting in', Math.round(delay / 1000), 'seconds');\n133\t\n134\t        state.reconnectTimer = setTimeout(function() {\n135\t            state.reconnectTimer = null;\n136\t            connectWebSocket();\n137\t        }, delay);\n138\t    }\n139\t\n140\t    function handleMessage(data) {\n141\t        try {\n142\t            const msg = JSON.parse(data);\n143\t\n144\t            // Handle snapshot (first message)\n145\t            if (msg.type === 'snapshot') {\n146\t                handleSnapshot(msg);\n147\t                return;\n148\t            }\n149\t\n150\t            // Handle incremental updates\n151\t            if (msg.blobs) updateBlobs(msg.blobs);\n152\t            if (msg.zones) updateZones(msg.zones);\n153\t            if (msg.nodes) updateNodes(msg.nodes);\n154\t            if (msg.events) updateEvents(msg.events);\n155\t            if (msg.alerts) updateAlerts(msg.alerts);\n156\t            if (msg.confidence !== undefined) state.system.detection_quality = msg.confidence;\n157\t            if (msg.security_mode !== undefined) {\n158\t                state.system.security_mode = msg.security_mode;\n159\t                updateSecurityButton();\n160\t            }\n161\t\n162\t            updateSystemStatus();\n163\t        } catch (e) {\n164\t            console.error('[Simple Mode] Error handling message:', e);\n165\t        }\n166\t    }\n167\t\n168\t    function handleSnapshot(msg) {\n169\t        state.blobs = msg.blobs || [];\n170\t        state.zones = msg.zones || [];\n171\t        state.nodes = msg.nodes || [];\n172\t        state.events = msg.events || [];\n173\t        state.alerts = msg.alerts || [];\n174\t        state.system.detection_quality = msg.confidence || 0;\n175\t        state.system.security_mode = msg.security_mode || false;\n176\t        state.system.nodes_online = (msg.nodes || []).filter(n => n.status === 'online').length;\n177\t        state.system.nodes_total = (msg.nodes || []).length;\n178\t\n179\t        renderAll();\n180\t        loadSleepSummary();\n181\t    }\n182\t\n183\t    // ============================================\n184\t    // Data Updates\n185\t    // ============================================\n186\t    function updateBlobs(blobs) {\n187\t        // Replace or add blobs by ID\n188\t        const ids = {};\n189\t        for (let i = 0; i < blobs.length; i++) {\n190\t            ids[blobs[i].id] = blobs[i];\n191\t        }\n192\t        state.blobs = state.blobs.filter(function(b) { return !(b.id in ids); });\n193\t        state.blobs = state.blobs.concat(blobs);\n194\t        renderZoneCards();\n195\t    }\n196\t\n197\t    function updateZones(zones) {\n198\t        const ids = {};\n199\t        for (let i = 0; i < zones.length; i++) {\n200\t            ids[zones[i].id] = zones[i];\n201\t        }\n202\t        state.zones = state.zones.filter(function(z) { return !(z.id in ids); });\n203\t        state.zones = state.zones.concat(zones);\n204\t        renderZoneCards();\n205\t    }\n206\t\n207\t    function updateNodes(nodes) {\n208\t        state.nodes = nodes;\n209\t        state.system.nodes_online = nodes.filter(n => n.status === 'online').length;\n210\t        state.system.nodes_total = nodes.length;\n211\t        updateSystemStatus();\n212\t    }\n213\t\n214\t    function updateEvents(events) {\n215\t        // Add new events to the beginning\n216\t        state.events = events.concat(state.events);\n217\t        // Keep only the most recent events\n218\t        if (state.events.length > CONFIG.MAX_EVENTS) {\n219\t            state.events = state.events.slice(0, CONFIG.MAX_EVENTS);\n220\t        }\n221\t        renderActivityFeed();\n222\t    }\n223\t\n224\t    function updateAlerts(alerts) {\n225\t        state.alerts = alerts || [];\n226\t        renderAlertBanner();\n227\t    }\n228\t\n229\t    // ============================================\n230\t    // Rendering\n231\t    // ============================================\n232\t    function renderAll() {\n233\t        renderZoneCards();\n234\t        renderActivityFeed();\n235\t        renderAlertBanner();\n236\t        updateSecurityButton();\n237\t        updateSystemStatus();\n238\t    }\n239\t\n240\t    function renderZoneCards() {\n241\t        if (!dom.zonesGrid) return;\n242\t\n243\t        if (state.zones.length === 0) {\n244\t            dom.zonesGrid.innerHTML = '<p class=\"simple-zone-card simple-zone-card--loading\">No rooms configured yet.</p>';\n245\t            return;\n246\t        }\n247\t\n248\t        const html = state.zones.map(function(zone) {\n249\t            const occupancy = zone.count || 0;\n250\t            const people = zone.people || [];\n251\t            const isOccupied = occupancy > 0;\n252\t            const hasAlert = zoneHasAlert(zone);\n253\t\n254\t            let statusClass = 'simple-zone-card--empty';\n255\t            if (hasAlert) {\n256\t                statusClass = 'simple-zone-card--alert';\n257\t            } else if (isOccupied) {\n258\t                statusClass = 'simple-zone-card--occupied';\n259\t            }\n260\t\n261\t            let statusText = isOccupied ?\n262\t                (occupancy === 1 ? '1 person' : occupancy + ' people') :\n263\t                'Empty';\n264\t\n265\t            let peopleHtml = '';\n266\t            if (people.length > 0) {\n267\t                peopleHtml = '<div class=\"simple-zone-card__people\">' +\n268\t                    people.map(function(p) {\n269\t                        return '<span class=\"simple-zone-card__person\">' + escapeHtml(p) + '</span>';\n270\t                    }).join('') +\n271\t                    '</div>';\n272\t            }\n273\t\n274\t            return '<div class=\"simple-zone-card ' + statusClass + '\" data-zone-id=\"' + zone.id + '\">' +\n275\t                '<div class=\"simple-zone-card__name\">' + escapeHtml(zone.name) + '</div>' +\n276\t                '<div class=\"simple-zone-card__status\">' + statusText + '</div>' +\n277\t                peopleHtml +\n278\t                '</div>';\n279\t        }).join('');\n280\t\n281\t        dom.zonesGrid.innerHTML = html;\n282\t\n283\t        // Add click handlers for zone cards\n284\t        dom.zonesGrid.querySelectorAll('.simple-zone-card').forEach(function(card) {\n285\t            card.addEventListener('click', function() {\n286\t                const zoneId = this.getAttribute('data-zone-id');\n287\t                showZoneActivity(zoneId);\n288\t            });\n289\t        });\n290\t    }\n291\t\n292\t    function zoneHasAlert(zone) {\n293\t        // Check if any active alerts are for this zone\n294\t        return state.alerts.some(function(alert) {\n295\t            return alert.zone === zone.name && !alert.acknowledged;\n296\t        });\n297\t    }\n298\t\n299\t    function renderActivityFeed() {\n300\t        if (!dom.activityFeed) return;\n301\t\n302\t        if (state.events.length === 0) {\n303\t            dom.activityFeed.innerHTML = '<p class=\"simple-feed__empty\">No recent activity</p>';\n304\t            return;\n305\t        }\n306\t\n307\t        const html = state.events.slice(0, 20).map(function(event) {\n308\t            return renderEventItem(event);\n309\t        }).join('');\n310\t\n311\t        dom.activityFeed.innerHTML = html;\n312\t    }\n313\t\n314\t    function renderEventItem(event) {\n315\t        const icon = getEventIcon(event.type);\n316\t        const title = getEventTitle(event);\n317\t        const time = formatTime(event.timestamp_ms);\n318\t        const zone = event.zone ? '<span class=\"simple-feed-item__zone\">' + escapeHtml(event.zone) + '</span>' : '';\n319\t\n320\t        return '<div class=\"simple-feed-item\" data-event-id=\"' + event.id + '\">' +\n321\t            '<div class=\"simple-feed-item__icon\">' + icon + '</div>' +\n322\t            '<div class=\"simple-feed-item__content\">' +\n323\t                '<div class=\"simple-feed-item__title\">' + escapeHtml(title) + '</div>' +\n324\t                '<div class=\"simple-feed-item__meta\">' +\n325\t                    '<span class=\"simple-feed-item__time\">' + time + '</span>' +\n326\t                    zone +\n327\t                '</div>' +\n328\t            '</div>' +\n329\t            '</div>';\n330\t    }\n331\t\n332\t    function getEventIcon(type) {\n333\t        const icons = {\n334\t            'detection': '&#x1F464;', // person\n335\t            'zone_entry': '&#x27A1;', // arrow right\n336\t            'zone_exit': '&#x2B05;', // arrow left\n337\t            'portal_crossing': '&#x2744;', // snowflake\n338\t            'trigger_fired': '&#x26A1;', // high voltage\n339\t            'fall_alert': '&#x26A0;', // warning\n340\t            'anomaly': '&#x1F515;', // radio\n341\t            'security_alert': '&#x1F512;', // lock\n342\t            'node_online': '&#x1F4E1;', // antenna\n343\t            'node_offline': '&#x1F4E5;', // crossed antenna\n344\t            'system': '&#x2699;', // gear\n345\t            'learning': '&#x1F4D6;' // book\n346\t        };\n347\t        return icons[type] || '&#x1F4AC;'; // speech bubble\n348\t    }\n349\t\n350\t    function getEventTitle(event) {\n351\t        if (event.person) {\n352\t            return event.person + ' — ' + (event.title || event.type);\n353\t        }\n354\t        return event.title || formatEventType(event.type);\n355\t    }\n356\t\n357\t    function formatEventType(type) {\n358\t        return type.replace(/_/g, ' ').replace(/\\b\\w/g, function(l) {\n359\t            return l.toUpperCase();\n360\t        });\n361\t    }\n362\t\n363\t    function formatTime(timestampMs) {\n364\t        const diff = Date.now() - timestampMs;\n365\t        if (diff < 60000) return 'just now';\n366\t        if (diff < 3600000) return Math.floor(diff / 60000) + 'm ago';\n367\t        if (diff < 86400000) return Math.floor(diff / 3600000) + 'h ago';\n368\t        return new Date(timestampMs).toLocaleDateString();\n369\t    }\n370\t\n371\t    function renderAlertBanner() {\n372\t        if (!dom.alertBanner) return;\n373\t\n374\t        // Check if alerts are silenced\n375\t        if (state.silencedUntil && Date.now() < state.silencedUntil) {\n376\t            dom.alertBanner.hidden = true;\n377\t            return;\n378\t        }\n379\t\n380\t        // Find the highest priority unacknowledged alert\n381\t        const alert = state.alerts.find(function(a) { return !a.acknowledged; });\n382\t\n383\t        if (!alert) {\n384\t            dom.alertBanner.hidden = true;\n385\t            return;\n386\t        }\n387\t\n388\t        dom.alertTitle.textContent = alert.title || 'Alert';\n389\t        dom.alertMessage.textContent = Show silence button if there are multiple alerts\n394\t        dom.silenceBtn.hidden = state.alerts.filter(a => !a.acknowledged).length <= 1;\n395\t    }\n396\t\n397\t    function updateSecurityButton() {\n398\t        if (!dom.securityBtn || !dom.securityLabel) return;\n399\t\n400\t        if (state.system.security_mode) {\n401\t            dom.securityLabel.textContent = 'Disarm Security';\n402\t            dom.securityBtn.classList.add('simple-action-btn--active');\n403\t        } else {\n404\t            dom.securityLabel.textContent = 'Arm Security';\n405\t            dom.securityBtn.classList.remove('simple-action-btn--active');\n406\t        }\n407\t    }\n408\t\n409\t    function updateSystemStatus() {\n410\t        if (!dom.systemStatus) return;\n411\t\n412\t        const quality = state.system.detection_quality;\n413\t        const nodes = state.system.nodes_online + '/' + state.system.nodes_total;\n414\t\n415\t        let status = 'System: ' + nodes + ' nodes online';\n416\t        if (quality > 0) {\n417\t            status += ' • ' + quality + '% quality';\n418\t        }\n419\t\n420\t        dom.systemStatus.textContent = status;\n421\t    }\n422\t\n423\t    function updateConnectionStatus(status) {\n424\t        if (!dom.connectionStatus) return;\n425\t\n426\t        const dot = dom.connectionStatus.querySelector('.simple-status__dot');\n427\t        const text = dom.connectionStatus.querySelector('.simple-status__text');\n428\t\n429\t        if (status === 'connected') {\n430\t            dot.className = 'simple-status__dot simple-status__dot--connected';\n431\t            text.textContent = 'Connected';\n432\t        } else if (status === 'connecting') {\n433\t            dot.className = 'simple-status__dot simple-status__dot--connecting';\n434\t            text.textContent = 'Connecting...';\n435\t        } else {\n436\t            dot.className = 'simple-status__dot simple-status__dot--disconnected';\n437\t            text.textContent = 'Disconnected — Reconnecting...';\n438\t        }\n439\t    }\n440\t\n441\t    // ============================================\n442\t    // Actions\n443\t    // ============================================\n444\t    function handleSecurityToggle() {\n445\t        const newState = !state.system.security_mode;\n446\t\n447\t        fetch('/api/security/' + (newState ? 'arm' : 'disarm'), {\n448\t            method: 'POST',\n449\t            headers: {\n450\t                'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n451\t            }\n452\t        }).then(function(response) {\n453\t            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to toggle security mode');\n454\t            return response.json();\n455\t        }).then(function(data) {\n456\t            state.system.security_mode = data.security_mode;\n457\t            updateSecurityButton();\n458\t            showToast(newState ? 'Security mode armed' : 'Security mode disarmed', 'success');\n459\t        }).catch(function(error) {\n460\t            console.error('[Simple Mode] Error toggling security:', error);\n461\t            showToast('Failed to toggle security mode', 'error');\n462\t        });\n463\t    }\n464\t\n465\t    function handleRebaseline() {\n466\t        fetch('/api/nodes/rebaseline-all', {\n467\t            method: 'POST',\n468\t            headers: {\n469\t                'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n470\t            }\n471\t        }).then(function(response) {\n472\t            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to trigger re-baseline');\n473\t            return response.json();\n474\t        }).then(function(data) {\n475\t            showToast('Re-baseline started — this takes about 60 seconds', 'info');\n476\t        }).catch(function(error) {\n477\t            console.error('[Simple Mode] Error triggering re-baseline:', error);\n478\t            showToast('Failed to trigger re-baseline', 'error');\n479\t        });\n480\t    }\n481\t\n482\t    function handleSilenceAlerts() {\n483\t        // Silence for 1 hour\n484\t        state.silencedUntil = Date.now() + 3600000;\n485\t        renderAlertBanner();\n486\t        showToast('Alerts silenced for 1 hour', 'info');\n487\t    }\n488\t\n489\t    function handleModeToggle() {\n490\t        // Save preference to localStorage\n491\t        localStorage.setItem(CONFIG.STORAGE_KEY_MODE, 'expert');\n492\t        // Navigate to expert mode\n493\t        window.location.href = '/live';\n494\t    }\n495\t\n496\t    function showZoneActivity(zoneId) {\n497\t        // Filter activity feed to show only events for this zone\n498\t        const zone = state.zones.find(function(z) { return z.id == zoneId; });\n499\t        if (!zone) return;\n500\t\n501\t        state.filters.zone = zone.name;\n502\t\n503\t        const filteredEvents = state.events.filter(function(e) {\n504\t            return e.zone === zone.name;\n505\t        });\n506\t\n507\t        if (filteredEvents.length === 0) {\n508\t            dom.activityFeed.innerHTML = '<p class=\"simple-feed__empty\">No recent activity in ' + escapeHtml(zone.name) + '</p>';\n509\t            return;\n510\t        }\n511\t\n512\t        const html = filteredEvents.slice(0, 20).map(function(event) {\n513\t            return renderEventItem(event);\n514\t        }).join('');\n515\t\n516\t        dom.activityFeed.innerHTML = html;\n517\t    }\n518\t\n519\t    // ============================================\n520\t    // Sleep Summary\n521\t    // ============================================\n522\t    function loadSleepSummary() {\n523\t        fetch('/api/sleep/summary')\n524\t            .then(function(response) {\n525\t                if (!response.ok) return null;\n526\t                return response.json();\n527\t            })\n528\t            .then(function(data) {\n529\t                if (!data || !data.date) {\n530\t                    if (dom.sleepCard) dom.sleepCard.hidden = true;\n531\t                    return;\n532\t                }\n533\t\n534\t                state.sleepData = data;\n535\t                renderSleepSummary();\n536\t            })\n537\t            .catch(function(error) {\n538\t                console.error('[Simple Mode] Error loading sleep summary:', error);\n539\t            });\n540\t    }\n541\t\n542\t    function renderSleepSummary() {\n543\t        if (!dom.sleepCard || !dom.sleepContent || !state.sleepData) return;\n544\t\n545\t        const data = state.sleepData;\n546\t        const html =\n547\t            '<p><strong>' + (data.duration_min ? Math.floor(data.duration_min / 60) + 'h ' + (data.duration_min % 60) + 'm' : 'N/A') +\n548\t            ' in bed</strong></p>' +\n549\t            '<p>Restlessness: ' + getRestlessnessLabel(data.restlessness) + '</p>' +\n550\t            '<p>Breathing: ' + getBreathingRegularityLabel(data.breathing_regularity) + '</p>';\n551\t\n552\t        dom.sleepContent.innerHTML = html;\n553\t        dom.sleepCard.hidden = false;\n554\t    }\n555\t\n556\t    function getRestlessnessLabel(value) {\n557\t        if (!value) return 'N/A';\n558\t        if (value < 1) return '<span class=\"simple-sleep__good\">Low</span>';\n559\t        if (value < 3) return '<span class=\"simple-sleep__ok\">Moderate</span>';\n560\t        return '<span class=\"simple-sleep__poor\">High</span>';\n561\t    }\n562\t\n563\t    function getBreathingRegularityLabel(value) {\n564\t        if (!value) return 'N/A';\n565\t        if (value < 0.15) return '<span class=\"simple-sleep__good\">Regular</span>';\n566\t        if (value < 0.25) return '<span class=\"simple-sleep__ok\">Fair</span>';\n567\t        return '<span class=\"simple-sleep__poor\">Irregular</span>';\n568\t    }\n569\t\n570\t    // ============================================\n571\t    // Toast Notifications\n572\t    // ============================================\n573\t    function showToast(message, type) {\n574\t        const container = document.querySelector('.toast-container');\n575\t        if (!container) {\n576\t            // Create container if it doesn't exist\n577\t            const tc = document.createElement('div');\n578\t            tc.className = 'toast-container';\n579\t            document.body.appendChild(tc);\n580\t        }\n581\t\n582\t        const toast = document.createElement('div');\n583\t        toast.className = 'toast toast--' + (type || 'info');\n584\t        toast.textContent = message;\n585\t\n586\t        document.querySelector('.toast-container').appendChild(toast);\n587\t\n588\t        // Remove after 3 seconds\n589\t        setTimeout(function() {\n590\t            toast.style.animation = 'toast-out 0.3s ease-out forwards';\n591\t            setTimeout(function() {\n592\t                if (toast.parentNode) {\n593\t                    toast.parentNode.removeChild(toast);\n594\t                }\n595\t            }, 300);\n596\t        }, 3000);\n597\t    }\n598\t\n599\t    // ============================================\n600\t    // Utility Functions\n601\t    // ============================================\n602\t    function escapeHtml(text) {\n603\t        const div = document.createElement('div');\n604\t        div.textContent = text;\n605\t        return div.innerHTML;\n606\t    }\n607\t\n608\t    // ============================================\n609\t    // Event Bindings\n610\t    // ============================================\n611\t    function bindEvents() {\n612\t        if (dom.modeToggle) {\n613\t            dom.modeToggle.addEventListener('click', handleModeToggle);\n614\t        }\n615\t\n616\t        if (dom.securityBtn) {\n617\t            dom.securityBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSecurityToggle);\n618\t        }\n619\t\n620\t        if (dom.rebaselineBtn) {\n621\t            dom.rebaselineBtn.addEventListener('click', handleRebaseline);\n622\t        }\n623\t\n624\t        if (dom.silenceBtn) {\n625\t            dom.silenceBtn.addEventListener('click',
